         <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
         <div class="date-outer">
          <h2 class="date-header">
           <span>
            05 July 2014
           </span>
          </h2>
          <div class="date-posts">
           <div class="post-outer">
            <div class="post hentry" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
             <a name="4874420509994330138">
             </a>
             <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
              Swatches &amp; Review - 3 Dance Legend Wow Prism Spring shades
             </h3>
             <div class="post-header">
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-4874420509994330138" itemprop="articleBody">
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               Hi loves! I am back with another Dance Legend post today. Sorry I'm a bit late, but today is just one of those super lazy Saturdays ;-). These shades will make up for it I think.
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-aV7rEbaMU3g/U7gL-697HBI/AAAAAAAAB8Y/azzAx6kdX_M/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Spring-collage.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Spring chunky holo" border="0" height="426" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-aV7rEbaMU3g/U7gL-697HBI/AAAAAAAAB8Y/azzAx6kdX_M/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Spring-collage.PNG" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Spring chunky holo" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               Dance Legend Wow Prism is now a collection of 24 gorgeous chunky holo shades, since there were 6 new shades released last Spring. Of those 6 I have 3 to show you and oh my, these might even be better than
               <a href="http://www.lovevarnish.com/2014/03/dance-legend-wow-prism-review-swatches.html">
                the other 4
               </a>
               I showed you earlier this year! I'll talk about the formula with each individual shade but I can tell you I used Duri Rejuvacote for my base, 3 coats of each color and topped it with Glisten &amp; Glow HK Girl Top Coat.
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               Let's take a look!
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
               <a name="more">
               </a>
               <br/>
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <b>
                Dance Legend Beautiful Lie
               </b>
               is a periwinkle purple shade. This one had a better formula compared to the other 2, it wasn't thin or runny and I could have settles with 2 coats, but did 3 for consistency. The chunky holo shines brightest in this one and shows an almost linear flare. Gorgeous!
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-81sW1PsE6u0/U7gL57alwRI/AAAAAAAAB7g/6xQ_HsG4p0I/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Beautiful-Lie-1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Beautiful Lie" border="0" height="426" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-81sW1PsE6u0/U7gL57alwRI/AAAAAAAAB7g/6xQ_HsG4p0I/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Beautiful-Lie-1.jpg" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Beautiful Lie" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-dNtUW_mwLSU/U7gL5ym-tqI/AAAAAAAAB7c/xlyN_GA5nF4/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Beautiful-Lie-2.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Beautiful Lie" border="0" height="426" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-dNtUW_mwLSU/U7gL5ym-tqI/AAAAAAAAB7c/xlyN_GA5nF4/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Beautiful-Lie-2.jpg" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Beautiful Lie" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-R0Ev2RuJhso/U7gL6PdCrVI/AAAAAAAAB7s/6_XhYtGh9Vg/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Beautiful-Lie-4.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Beautiful Lie" border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-R0Ev2RuJhso/U7gL6PdCrVI/AAAAAAAAB7s/6_XhYtGh9Vg/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Beautiful-Lie-4.jpg" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Beautiful Lie" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <b>
                Dance Legend Holy Diver
               </b>
               is named appropriately, this mermaid like greenish turquoise has a mesmerizing depth to it! The chunky holo sparkles nicely, the formula is thin though and I think you might wanna double up on basecoat - this could be a stainer! Really make sure your brush doesn't have to much polish on it oir you'll flood your cuticles.
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MReK2ab0JdU/U7gL6lA9ltI/AAAAAAAAB8E/P2515R8DmY8/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Holy-Diver-1.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Holy Diver" border="0" height="426" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MReK2ab0JdU/U7gL6lA9ltI/AAAAAAAAB8E/P2515R8DmY8/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Holy-Diver-1.JPG" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Holy Diver" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-U2nlAlOaZQ4/U7gL6z1FuSI/AAAAAAAAB8M/qNIo9R5GYnk/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Holy-Diver-2.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Holy Diver" border="0" height="426" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-U2nlAlOaZQ4/U7gL6z1FuSI/AAAAAAAAB8M/qNIo9R5GYnk/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Holy-Diver-2.JPG" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Holy Diver" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-AvWynJevT6I/U7gL60efbrI/AAAAAAAAB8U/cNLDBiX00-I/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Holy-Diver-4.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Holy Diver" border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-AvWynJevT6I/U7gL60efbrI/AAAAAAAAB8U/cNLDBiX00-I/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Holy-Diver-4.JPG" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Holy Diver" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <b>
                Dance Legend Inhale
               </b>
               is a bright and clean green shade, this makes me think of plants and leafs! The holographic effect isn't the strongest with this one but the sparkling finish is still gorgeous. Again, thin formula and potential flooding of cuticles if you aren't careful with it. Worth it though!
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-v6Ue5X6Q1Pc/U7gL7dRsNuI/AAAAAAAAB74/8cxl7PUCpQ4/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Inhale-1.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Inhale" border="0" height="426" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-v6Ue5X6Q1Pc/U7gL7dRsNuI/AAAAAAAAB74/8cxl7PUCpQ4/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Inhale-1.JPG" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Inhale" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ohtCnFRJYGo/U7gL7i6GFRI/AAAAAAAAB8A/HDcj73EweHI/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Inhale-2.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Inhale" border="0" height="426" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ohtCnFRJYGo/U7gL7i6GFRI/AAAAAAAAB8A/HDcj73EweHI/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Inhale-2.JPG" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Inhale" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-e1TIBIhUJWY/U7gL8eSbIEI/AAAAAAAAB8I/xZgIm-iVmUk/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Inhale-4.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img alt="Dance Legend Wow Prism Inhale" border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-e1TIBIhUJWY/U7gL8eSbIEI/AAAAAAAAB8I/xZgIm-iVmUk/s1600/Dance-Legend-Wow-Prism-Inhale-4.JPG" title="Dance Legend Wow Prism Inhale" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: justify;">
               <b>
                That's it, my 3 picks from the Dance Legend Wow Prism Spring collection! Which shade would you choose? Tell me in the comments!
               </b>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: right;">
               <a class="button_example" href="http://www.lovevarnish.com/p/disclosure-policy.html" style="display: inline-block; text-decoration: none;">
